# Decisions scratchpad — autonomous calls for Alex to review

Running log of judgment calls made while you were away. Newest at the bottom.
Format: **D# — decision** · rationale · revisit?

---

**D1 — Setup action budget (64) + deterministic auto-fix.** Random/untrained agents livelock in the setup phase (can't randomly satisfy "exactly 11, 3+ on LoS, ≤2 per wide zone" and pick DONE). Real BB has setup clocks; FUMBBL enforces them. After 64 placement actions, only `SETUP_DONE` is legal and the engine deterministically repairs the formation (no dice → replay-safe). Full setup expressiveness retained below the budget. *Revisit:* budget size; whether RL policies should see a penalty signal for hitting autofix.

**D2 — `BB_LEGAL_MAX` = 4096.** Setup enumerates ~3000 player×square placements. The RL action heads never materialize this list (factored heads); it's for replay validation/fuzzing/tests. 16KB stack per enumeration is fine.

**D3 — Starter skill set in Phase 2 core** (loner, dodge, block, tackle, guard, thick_skull, stunty, sure_feet, sure_hands, pass, catch, sprint) wired through `bb_skills.h` hooks; everything else lands Phase 3 through the same hooks. Wrestle/Frenzy/Mighty Blow/apothecary deliberately deferred (decision windows not yet modeled) — each marked `TODO(phase3)` in source.

**D4 — Kickoff events: 4 of 11 implemented** (Time-Out, Brilliant Coaching, Changing Weather, Pitch Invasion); the decision-heavy ones (Solid Defence, Quick Snap, High Kick, Charge, Cheering Fans→prayers, Get the Ref→bribes, Dodgy Snack) are rule-shaped no-ops marked `TODO(phase3)`. Phase 4 differential validation will quantify the gap.

**D5 — Pass mechanics v1 approximations** (flagged for the rulebook-test campaign to correct): Euclidean range bands; natural-1≈fumble folded into the inaccurate path; interception deferred. The rulebook tests being written right now will force exactness; FUMBBL replays are the final word.

**D6 — Golden traces: 8 matchups committed** (incl. Ogre vs Snotling for stunty/big-guy coverage). Regenerating goldens is an explicit `make goldens` — rules fixes are EXPECTED to break goldens; that's their job.

**D7 — Vast.ai**: key stored at `~/.vast_api_key`, verified live ($96.26 credit). Spend capped at your authorized $50. No GPU spend until the PufferLib binding smoke test (Phase 5).

**D8 — GitHub remote deferred.** Repo is local-only so far; creating a private GH repo is outward-facing and can wait for your morning review (CI workflow file is ready to go when pushed).

**D9 — Wrestle auto-applies on Both Down.** Rules make it optional ("may choose"); since declining is almost never right and the rulebook tests expect auto-application, the engine applies it when either player has it. Revisit if FUMBBL replays show declines.
**D10 — Single-candidate interceptions auto-attempt.** Attempting is cost-free (no failure penalty), so with one eligible interceptor there's no real decision; with several, the defending coach chooses. Matches the rulebook tests.
**D11 — Crowd-push dice order.** Crowd injury + throw-in resolve at relocation time, BEFORE the follow-up decision — FFB's order, and what the blocking tests encode. GAME/FOLLOW-UP's "decision before any other dice" reading is a known minor divergence to check against FUMBBL replays.
**D12 — Pitch Invasion victim selection** uses the raw PRNG (not the scripted dice stream) — FUMBBL records selections as separate commands, so replay alignment handles it at the harness level. Fan-factor modifiers TODO with the fans/inducements work.
**D13 — Secure the Ball failure = bounce + turnover** (consistent with the failed-pickup family). Rule text doesn't settle it; flagged for FFB differential adjudication.
**D14 — Test-vs-test conflicts resolved toward the mirror**: throw-in direction die is a D6 over the 3 template arrows (corners: D3); distance counts the boundary square as the first; no bounce on an empty landing square. Two agent tests written with d3/full-distance/bounce assumptions were corrected.
**D15 — BB2025 team re-rolls are UNLIMITED per turn** (the BB2020 once-per-turn cap is gone) and replenish at half-time; skill re-rolls (Dodge/Sure Feet/...) are once per TURN per player. Engine restructured accordingly.
**D16 — Mighty Blow auto-policy.** MB(+1) is rules-wise a choice of armour OR injury roll. Engine auto-applies: to the armour roll only when that converts a miss into a break, otherwise to the injury roll — the strictly dominant line in >99% of cases (exception: fishing for specific injury bands). Claws+MB on the same roll disallowed per rules; Claws' 8+ auto-break consumes the slot. Revisit if FUMBBL replays show deviating choices.
**D17 — Stand Firm always-on** (no decline window; declining is never beneficial absent edge interactions). Same for auto-attempting cost-free single-candidate interceptions (D10).
**D18 — Kick auto-applies** (halve deviation) when any on-pitch kicking-team player has Kick — kicker nomination (not adjacent to LoS/wide zone) is folded into the fans/nomination TODO. **Break Tackle** is always-on per-dodge (rules: once per activation) — flagged for the FUMBBL differential. **Secret Weapon** send-off uses on-pitch-at-drive-end as "took part" approximation.
**D19 — Interrupt auto-policies.** Tentacles: every eligible tentacled marker attempts (cost-free, compulsory-shaped); one attempt per step. Diving Tackle: auto-applied when the -2 flips a passing dodge (the only rational use), never with a ball-carrying diver; first eligible marker dives. Shadowing still pending (needs per-turn MA-use counter). These become real decision windows if the RL action space wants them; FUMBBL differential will adjudicate fidelity.
**D20 — Apothecary casualty pick auto-selects the better band** (strictly dominant given equal in-match effect); KO-patch remains a real decision (saving the apo matters). Casualty outcomes now recorded in spp_game for league mode.
**D21 — More auto-policies (Drop B):** Trickster auto-relocates only when it fully escapes the blocker (else stays); Dump-Off auto-throws to the least-marked quick-range teammate; Saboteur always triggers (cost: auto-KO — debatable, FUMBBL will adjudicate); SPOH places in the first empty adjacent square; Solid Defence/Quick Snap/Charge roll their D3 for dice-stream fidelity but reposition no one yet (decision windows TODO); Dodgy Snack's stat debuff persists for the match (drive-end restoration comes with procedural squads); Bloodlust thrall-bite + Animosity keyword targeting need keyword data (gate fires on declaration as approximation). Multiple Block + Pile Driver deferred (no default-roster carriers).
**D22 — Phase 5 design pivot per policy research** (docs/policy-research.md): compact ~640B entity-centric obs (NOT board planes — 20GB rollout buffer at bf16 otherwise); ACT_SIZES {type, arg, fused-391-square} each with a null index; stock Linear→MinGRU×3 policy (config-only, ~3.8M params); env-phase decision decomposition (the engine already provides it).
**D23 — Decode snap-to-legal has a low-x bias under pure-random heads.** When all 3 sampled heads form an illegal combo and no same-type match exists, decode falls back to `legal[0]`; engine enumeration order biases that toward low-x squares, which favors the away team (perf 0.38-0.40 at 99.8% illegal, two seeds). Irrelevant under the CUDA masked sampler (per-head legality keeps illegal_frac near 0 and passes 1-2 respect type+square), and vanishes as the policy sharpens. Documented, not fixed — randomizing the fallback would cost a per-step RNG draw for a transient artifact.
**D24 — Mac practice-run path (torch backend).** Three Mac-only walls, all worked around without touching upstream semantics: (1) `SIMD_FLAGS=(-mavx2 -mfma)` is a hard error on arm64 clang — guarded in the gitignored vendored build.sh; (2) torch bundles its own libomp, homebrew's in `_C.so` makes two OpenMP runtimes → segfault in `__kmp_suspend_initialize_thread`; `tools/mac_practice_build.sh` builds _C WITHOUT -fopenmp (pragmas degrade to single-thread; vecenv uses no omp_* API); (3) the selfplay pool raises RuntimeError on non-CUDA backends and pufferl exits cleanly-but-silently → practice runs need `--selfplay.enabled 0`. Verified: 147.5K steps / 12 PPO epochs end-to-end on M-series CPU at 14.7K SPS, stats flowing, exit 0.
**D25 — Setup discipline (amends D1).** Reserves-first placement: until 11 are placed (or reserves exhausted), re-placing/removing placed players is illegal — the spectator showed undertrained policies shuffling one player between two squares for the whole budget. Every final formation stays reachable (fill the line, then rearrange). Budget 64→24. Side effect: setup's legal-action enumeration shrank ~15x, doubling whole-match throughput (176K→353K steps/sec/core standalone). Deployed AFTER the A/B runs (mid-experiment engine changes confound); profiles from round 2 (gamma ladder) onward use it.
**D26 — Bootstrap curriculum: stage-1 works, cold anneal fails.** Profile D (fetch/carry potentials, 10B) escaped the 0-0 avoidance basin both pure arms died in (tds 0→0.06 mid-run). Stage-2 cold anneal (D2: same weights, potentials hard-off) decayed back to tds 0.000 by 5.4B — the scoring behavior was scaffold-supported, not value-internalized. D2 cut at 5.4B (info value of the tail ~nil). Conclusions: curriculum needs GRADUAL anneal (e.g. halve potentials per chained stage) and/or much longer stage-1; the BC arm is the priority path. Both 10B checkpoints retained for puffer match baselines.
**D27 — Cross-population tournament (4096 games/match): the avoidance equilibrium is universal, and PPO erodes priors into it.** All cross-matches ≈100% draws (BC/A/D/BC-init — nobody scores on anybody). The one directly informative result: BC-init BEATS BC-final (0.510 in decisive games) — 10B steps of selfplay PPO made the human-derived policy strictly worse at football. Confirms the tds-decay reading: with win/TD rewards unreachable at this defensive skill level, the gradient prunes scoring behavior as wasted entropy. Indicated fixes, in order: (1) BC-regularized PPO (KL/aux-CE anchor to the human policy during RL — the AlphaStar solution); (2) gradual potential anneal (halve per stage, never cold-off); (3) asymmetric curriculum (train offense vs frozen weaker defense). Also fixed tonight: our Log now exports slot_0/slot_1/draw_rate so puffer match works at all.
**D28 — Gradual anneal GRADUATES: the curriculum works.** Chain (each 10B, warm-started): 50% potentials → tds 0.185 (record, still climbing at cutoff); 25% → 0.035 (sustained, no surge); 0% → 0.045 and GROWING all run (0.009→0.045). Control: D2's cold-cut died (0.000 by 5.4B) from a weaker base. Conclusion: scaffold-taught scoring consolidates into the value function when removed gradually — the true reward's event density at handoff is the survival condition. Caveats: selfplay tds is confounded (tournament arbitrates); the whole lineage trained under the [-1,1] reward clamp (D27 addendum — outcome hierarchy was distorted but potentials were unaffected); deep-setup habit fossil noted by Alex on the spectator (eval-suite metric added).
**D29 — D9 reversal scheduled: Wrestle becomes a real decision window.** Alex's counterexample to D9's auto-apply: a Wrestle defender vs a Block-less attacker should often DECLINE — plain Both-Down knocks the attacker down (turnover for the attacking team) at the cost of mutual armour rolls; using Wrestle safely places both prone with no turnover. State-dependent trade ⇒ genuine decision. Fix (obs-v3/engine cycle): USE_SKILL/DECLINE_SKILL window for the owner at Both-Down; FUMBBL skillUse reports validate via lockstep AND feed BC pairs for the judgment. Probability engine: choice nodes resolve owner-optimally. Principle recorded: every "may" in the rulebook is policy surface; auto-policies delete tactics.
**D31 — Cycle-2 engine windows landed (D29/D17/D20/D21 reversals + divergence fixes).** Wrestle (attacker-then-defender USE/DECLINE windows at Both Down, FFB StepWrestle order), Stand Firm (decline window on every push incl. chains; chain-occupant stand-firm now absorbs the parent push in place), apothecary casualty patch-up (real CHOOSE_OPTION between the two D16 results), negatrait gates (roll AFTER declaring; Really Stupid +2 helper; Unchannelled Fury +2 on Block/Blitz; Take Root standing-only; failed gates offer the team re-roll window with the Loner gate), kickoff windows (Solid Defence re-setup incl. off-pitch staging, Quick Snap one-square steps, Charge! free activations through the real ACTIVATION machinery with active-team handover + turnover-as-event-end), Changing Weather gust rolls per-die and stops at the touchback boundary (FFB; the mirror's flat Scatter (3) over-rolls when the ball exits early), Pick-Me-Up rolls after the boundary stun roll-over with helper snapshot, Pitch Invasion adds Fan Factor (new `bb_match.fan_factor[2]` — **engine_fp changed; the demo-state bank must be regenerated**), and the inverted Defensive-cancels-Guard turn check is fixed (item 11 root cause; residual nrOfDice cases are FFB star specials like Gored By The Bull's extra block die, not modelled). Deferred: Kick-off Return (FUMBBL BB2020-ruleset relic — absent from the BB2025 mirror, stays a classified mapper divergence), Charge! up-front selection (we check Open lazily at activation time), TTM/KTM dice mapping (mapper-side; charge TTM activations drop classified). *Revisit:* none — every "may" here is now policy surface per D29's principle.

**D30 — Heterogeneous league alone: universal robustness, zero offense.** League v1 (5 seeded styles, winrate-gated swaps, clamp-fixed rewards, graduate warm start, 10B): final winrates exactly 0.50 vs ALL five banks (wall/D/BC-init/stage-1/graduate); zero earned swaps; own tds eroded 0.027→0.000. With D26/D27/D28: the mechanism quartet is now fully isolated — scaffold teaches skill, gradual anneal retains it, league diversity hardens it, anchor (box-2: bc_acc 0.93, tds 0.45 mid-run) preserves it. None sufficient alone ⇒ cycle 2 = the synthesis run (anchor + league + drills + obs-v3 + D29/D21 windows + 58K-pair corpus).
**D32 — Anchored-PPO partial result (cut at ~2.5B for the synthesis cutover).** BC-regularized PPO (24K-pair anchor, cosine-annealed): sustained bc_acc 0.93-0.96 and tds 0.39-0.45 through 2.5B steps even at the bc_coef floor (0.1) — an order of magnitude above every unanchored arm, no erosion. The anchor thesis is confirmed; full-length validation folds into the synthesis run (bc_v2, 70K pairs, obs-v3).
**D33 — blocks 0.000 on the synthesis run is REAL behavior, not a broken counter — and the mechanism is quantified.** Suspicion: bc_acc 0.80 (teacher-forced, on human pairs full of blocks) with on-policy blocks 0.000 looked like instrument failure. Probe (puffer/bloodbowl/bbe_microstats_probe.c, masked-random policy, 200 eps): blocks 1.875/ep, blitzes 6.14/ep — the counter ticks fine under any non-degenerate policy; verified wired at c_step→bbe_count_action on every applied decision. So the synthesis policy has actively zeroed block declarations. WHY: the same probe shows random contact is net self-harm — kd_own 1.75 vs kd_inflicted 0.61 (~3:1 against). PPO descends that gradient immediately ("all blocks bad") and cannot climb to "selective 2dB-with-Block blocks are +EV" — a textbook shaping valley, exactly Alex's spectator observation. The BC anchor doesn't prevent it: block declarations are a thin slice of the pair distribution, so the policy keeps 0.80 aggregate accuracy while zeroing them on-policy (knowledge-behavior gap; anchor CE is state-averaged, not behavior-coverage-weighted). Implications: (1) Profile C decision-time exposure pricing (k_kd × P(knockdown) etc. — spec in docs/reward-audit-decision-time.md Addendum 3, 2dB(2.8%)-vs-3d(3.7%) inversion test) is now empirically motivated, not just theorized — ungated. (2) Candidate anchor upgrade: weight BC loss by decision type (or oversample DECLARE pairs) so block judgment transfers; pairs already carry the action type. (3) Eval-suite metric: blocks/ep on demo-started episodes is the cleanest "does it fight when it should" probe.
**D34 — Profile C cures the never-blocking meta in one from-scratch 10B run.** First live run of the exposure-EV transfer (bb_blockev closed forms; k_kd 0.06 / k_value 0.5 / k_ball 0.3 / k_seq 0.02; native CUDA, 2.6M SPS — EV overhead unmeasurable): blocks 6.7/ep + blitzes 10.6/ep vs 0.000 on EVERY previously trained policy (D33; random baseline 1.9+6.1). Knockdown conversion 23%/declaration vs random's 7.5% — the zero-sum transfer teaches target selection from both sides as the spec predicted. Behavioral arc within the run: early 8.8 blocks/7.2 blitzes → final 6.7/10.6 — the policy discovered blitzes (choose your engagement) dominate static blocks. Declaration volume ~17/ep is BELOW human range (~15-30 blocks/game/team), so no farming; ep_return 0.336 (setup + seq-charge residue) stable across 10B. tds 0.000 — expected and out of scope: exposure pricing cures combat avoidance, not the scoring basin (D26-D28's territory). Caveats: selfplay symmetry forces inflicted:own ≈ 1:1, so attrition VOLUME/conversion are the claims, not net attrition; block-seeking vs positioning tension untested until scoring pressure exists. NEXT: synthesis+C on box-2 when the synthesis run completes (anchor + demos + drills + exposure — first run with both the scoring lineage and combat pricing); C checkpoint (1780628253178) retained as a "brawler" league seed style the pool lacked.
**D35 — bc_v3: the 1M-pair anchor (corpus scale-up pays).** Scraper corpus 401 → 5,748 curated replays; normalize+extract held yield exactly (177.9 pairs/replay vs 175.1) → 1,022,549 pairs / 2.1 GB. bc_v3 (12K steps, batch 1024, split BY REPLAY): val exact 0.360 vs bc_v2's 0.324 (+3.6pp), type/arg/sq 0.906/0.834/0.562 — and val ≈ train (0.373) at this scale, i.e. the model is now capacity-bound, not data-bound: the next anchor jump comes from a bigger policy or sequence context (the known iid-BC limitation), not more replays. Ops notes: bc_pretrain's post-save CUDA-blob convert needs a --float _C (box-1 is bf16-native — convert on box-2 instead); box-to-box rsync works with ssh-add + agent forwarding (auth happens once at connect; the transfer survives the launcher session). bc_v3.bin + full pair corpus staged on box-2: synthesis+C (run_synthesis_c.sh) auto-picks it as the freshest anchor and the bc-reg loader sees the full corpus.
**D36 — Adversarial panel over the Profile C stack (95 agents, 30 findings → 21 confirmed / 9 refuted) + the fix cycle.** Run before committing synthesis+C to 10B (workflow wf_13fb2bd1; full findings archived in the panel output). Fixed in this cycle: (1) HIGH rush-gated blitz pricing — exposure now scales by P(rush succeeds) and the sequencing charge folds the rush-failure turnover (with the Steady Footing save); the unscaled version paid attackers up to ~0.17/turn of fictitious zero-sum reward for doomed max-range blitzes — half of D34's entire observed ep_return. (2) D16 AMENDED: Claws checked BEFORE Mighty Blow and a Claws break leaves MB for the injury roll (the "MB cannot stack with Claws" comment had no rulebook basis); MB+Claws removal 285→315/1296 at AV9 and the Claws→high-AV gradient un-inverted (AV11 now equals AV9 at 315 instead of reading WORSE at 243). (3) Sure Hands now blocks Strip Ball (mirror clause; engine + EV; every Thrower/Runner archetype carries it — p_ball_out was overpriced 5/6 vs 3/6). (4) EV drift fixes: Juggernaut-blitz cancels Stand Firm in strip_fires; Fend (non-Juggernaut) cancels the Frenzy second block (~8pp p_def_down overprice gone); Cheering Fans latch consumed once; Brawler's mandatory Both-Down auto-reroll modeled exactly via a full 6^nd pool-enumeration rewrite of eval_pool (replaces the rank formula; equivalent where both apply, verified by the suite). (5) Counters: blocks_thrown (one CHOOSE_DIE per resolved block) added as the clean conversion denominator; Charge! free blitzes exempted from the sequencing charge; player_cost/value-scaled-injury lookups bounds-clamped and the demo-bank loader validates record index bytes. (6) Launch hardening: ANCHOR pinned to bc_v3.bin with size sanity (dead-lineage glob mis-resolution), demo bank existence+size verified (missing bank was SILENT procgen-only), 40s liveness check. Validation: 337 tests green; MC differential extended 18→25 matchups (MB+Claws, Sure Hands, Juggernaut-SF, Brawler ×2, Fend, 2d Frenzy) with per-block policy recomputation — zero drift. Engine-parity divergences from the mirror DOCUMENTED not fixed (engine and EV agree; FUMBBL differential will adjudicate): Frenzy-vs-Steady-Footing missing second block (≤5.6% pool mass), Dump-Off dead once-latch. Refuted by the panel's own refuters (worth recording): B-knobs-atop-C is NOT double-pricing (audit table holds), the clamp is not breached by any realistic step in this config.
**D34 AMENDED (control run): "cures the never-blocking meta" → "creates contact-seeking".** The panel demanded a matched control: from-scratch, identical config/backend, k-knobs zeroed, 1.5B steps. Result: blocks 2.56 + blitzes 6.15/ep ≈ the masked-random baseline (8.0 contact/ep), kd_inflicted 1.08/ep — i.e. WITHOUT C, from-scratch contact never moves off random; it neither collapses (that's a property of the shaped/anchored lineages, D33) nor grows. Profile C at the same scale: ~16-17 contact/ep with 3.5-4.1 kd/ep. Corrected claim: shaped lineages collapse contact to zero; unshaped from-scratch leaves it at random; ONLY the exposure transfer creates contact-seeking (~2x random volume, ~2x per-declaration conversion even against the control). The 23%-vs-7.5% conversion comparison in D34's original text used declaration denominators (panel: blitz declarations that never reach a block deflate the random side) — blocks_thrown now exists for clean future comparisons.
**D33 AMENDED (scope): the 3:1 self-harm ratio is contact-PLUS-movement risk, not block EV.** kd_own pools failed dodges/GFIs/surfs with block self-downs, and window-owner attribution books an attacker's against-dice skulls (defender picks the die) into the DEFENDER'S kd_inflicted. The corrected reading of D33: "acting at random is net self-harm, and PPO prunes ALL initiations — contact first" (the conclusion stands; the mechanism number was never block-specific). The D34 control's kd 1.08/ep at random-level contact is the cleaner baseline going forward.
**D35 AMENDED: "capacity-bound" downgraded to "variance-gap closed" pending the optimization-bound check.** val≈train cannot distinguish capacity from under-training: bc_v3 saw only ~15 epochs at constant LR (bc_v2's identical step budget = ~175 epochs of its smaller corpus — the +3.6pp "corpus gain" is epoch-confounded and likely UNDERSTATES the corpus benefit). bc_v3b (resume +30K steps, cosine decay — bc_pretrain.py grew --init/--cosine) is running; if train-exact climbs past 0.373 the next anchor investment is more steps, not a bigger model.
**D35 VERDICT (optimization-bound check): the panel was right.** bc_v3b = bc_v3 + 30K cosine-decay steps on the same corpus: train exact 0.373→0.406, VAL 0.360→0.371 (+1.1pp of real held-out gain the "capacity-bound" reading said could not exist). The train-val gap (0.406 vs 0.371) has now genuinely opened — THIS is the capacity/variance frontier, reached by optimizing properly, not asserted from a budget artifact. bc_v3b is the synthesis+C anchor (pinned in run_synthesis_c.sh); next anchor levers in order: sequence context > bigger policy > more data.
**D37 — Host reboot ends synthesis-v4 at 5.8B; early handoff to synthesis+C.** Vast host power-cycled at ~14:48 PDT 2026-06-05 (uptime evidence; container overlay survived, all processes died — the armed handoff watcher included). Verdict on synthesis-v4 (5.8B of 10B): the thesis result is in — bc_acc 0.69→0.978 monotone, tds stable 0.37-0.61 with ZERO decay through 5.8B (previous best: D32's 2.5B partial; every unanchored arm: dead by 3B). The remaining 4.2B was confirmation, not information; its checkpoints (~58, through 5.8B) survive on-box + Mac-synced for the tournament. SYNTHESIS+C LAUNCHED 15:35 PDT via the hardened script, all gates green: bc_v3b anchor, 1,022,549-pair BC loss (dashboard bc_acc starts 0.378 ≈ bc_v3b's full-corpus exact — the 1M-pair target is honest, unlike the old memorized 24K set), 15,471-state bank functioning (demo_episodes ~0.45, fallbacks 0.000), B-knobs + k_kd/k_value/k_ball/k_seq with the D36 rush gating, 114K SPS (fresh-boot bonus vs 54-90K). THE SIGNAL to read at ~1B: tds holds ~0.4+ AND blocks_thrown departs zero — gates fleet wave 1 (docs/fleet-playbook.md).
**D38 — THE UNMASKED-SAMPLER BUG: the torch backend never applied action masks; every BC-anchored run played via decode fallback (illegal_frac 1.000).** Found chasing synthesis+C's blocks 0.000 AND blitzes 0.000 at 200M (exact zeros — structure, not behavior). Mechanism: bc_pretrain (and the bc_acc aux loss) train/score MASK-RESTRICTED logits; the torch backend samples RAW logits (masks were CUDA-only); the BC policy never had to learn raw-logit legality, so on-policy it sampled ~100% illegal and bbe_decode's fallback (same-type → legal[0]) played a MOVE-biased shadow policy. Measured: bc_v3b lr~0 probe — unmasked: illegal 0.999, blocks 0.000, blitzes 0.000; MASKED: illegal 0.235 (residual = joint arg×sq misses across independent head masks), blocks 12.4/ep, blocks_thrown 13.6/ep, blitzes 2.8/ep — HUMAN-RANGE contact from the same weights. Fix (training/torch_pufferl_bcreg.patch + puffer_dict_capacity.patch regenerated): bindings expose vec action_mask (cpu+gpu); torch_pufferl applies per-head masked_fill(-inf) BEFORE rollout sampling, stores masks in experience, and re-applies at train-time recompute (mask-consistent ratios/entropy; all-zero head row guard). REINTERPRETATIONS: D33's knowledge-behavior gap = largely this artifact; D32/synthesis-v4 "anchor holds" results stand as experiments but measured fallback-shadow dynamics (their tds/pickups arose through legal[0]-snapping, with PPO slowly re-learning legality in raw logits); the avoidance-basin conclusions (D26-D28, CUDA, masked) unaffected; D34's Profile C result (CUDA, masked) unaffected. Unmasked synthesis+C control killed at ~300M (preserved in log); SYNTHESIS+C-MASKED relaunched 16:25 PDT — the first torch run whose behavior and knowledge share a distribution. Viewer inherits the fix (same patch) — on-screen play is now the real policy.
**D39 — Masked-world 1B read: contact learned, winning not (yet); fleet wave gated to the morning.** synthesis+C-masked at ~1B: blocks_thrown 13.6 (bc_v3b prior) → 34-43/ep, knockdowns 15-19/ep, blitzes 27 — the exposure transfer expresses immediately and PPO amplifies it; tds 0.000 (one 0.011 flicker at 357M); bc_acc ~0.39 ≈ 96% of bc_v3b's honest full-corpus ceiling (0.406) — the "rising bc_acc" signature of the fallback era is impossible by design now. Tournament arbitration (4096 games, CUDA, both sides bias-drop-converted): cm-1B vs bc_v3b-init = 97.4% draws, decisive split 48.7/51.3 — NO win-rate progress; the brawling is profitable but not instrumental. Interpretation: with masked sampling the true difficulty surfaced — the old runs' tds ~0.5 was scored against fallback shadow-defense, so all prior tds-emergence intuitions need rebasing. Plan: cook to ~3.5B overnight (D26/D28 precedent: emergence at 1-3B; bc-coef cosine relaxes the anchor); morning gate: tds ~0 → relaunch with k_kd/k_value/k_ball/k_seq HALVED and launch the fleet k-grid (the dense-exposure-vs-sparse-objective gradient competition is now the sharpest open question); tds climbing → wave on current config.
**D40 — Gate fired at 3.4B: full-k masked plateau confirmed; halved-k arm launched.** synthesis+C-masked rode a perfectly stable equilibrium from ~0.4B to 3.4B: blocks_thrown 34-39/ep, knockdowns 15-19/ep, blitzes 25-27, bc_acc oscillating 0.38-0.41 (at the bc_v3b ceiling), illegal ~0.33, tds 0.000 sustained (two isolated flickers, 357M and 1.3B, never compounding) — plus the D39 tournament's no-win-progress verdict. Reading: the exposure transfer's dense gradient is fully harvested and the policy parked there; the sparse win/TD signal never got purchase. Per the pre-committed gate: relaunched 03:05 PDT from bc_v3b with k_kd 0.03 / k_value 0.25 / k_ball 0.15 / k_seq 0.01 (HALVED; tag profile-synthesis-ck, /tmp/synthesis_cmk.log). Full-k checkpoints retained (run dir 1780701942283) as the brawler-pole reference for the k-grid. Fleet k-grid provisioning deferred to daylight (3 AM unattended multi-box provisioning = zombie risk); morning read compares halved-k's first ~2B against the full-k curve.
**D41 — Wave 2 launched (the 3-arm masked-world experiment).** Per the morning read (halved-k found a different contact equilibrium ~29/ep vs full-k's 40, still tds 0 — knob magnitude moves the brawl pole, not scoring): (1) box-2 repurposed to the TRUE anneal chain — stage 2 warm-started from the full-k 3.4B checkpoint at half-k, 3B cap, then quarter→zero (D28 doctrine applied to exposure); the fresh constant-half run's 1.3B is retained as the mid-pole reference. (2) bb-kzero (48c 4090): anchor-only masked control — the missing baseline for whether exposure pricing HURTS scoring. (3) bb-ballhawk (64c 4090): Alex's super-ballhawk arm — anchor + dist_ball 0.1/sq + dist_endzone 0.2/sq (5x D-profile potentials, telescoping/unfarmable), no k-knobs: the offense pole, untested in the masked world where the original D-escape predates both masks and anchor. Bootstrap via new tools/setup_arm.sh. Corpus crossed 11,595 replays overnight.
**D42 — Ballhawk v1 postmortem (the scrum standoff) + the scrum-literate v2 (Alex's insight).** v1 (fetch 0.1/carry 0.2, k=0) at 3.4B on the 766K-SPS box: pickup_attempts COLLAPSED to 0.36/ep (vs ~1.0 baseline), gfi 17/ep, dodges 16.7, knockdowns_own 8.8, pass 0.000, tds 0.000, episode_return +0.67 — diagnosis: both teams sprint to the loose ball (fetch potential is side-symmetric), form a TZ forest around it, and HOVER — in-traffic pickup EV is deeply negative (-1/TZ, turnover on failure) and the potential income stops at adjacency. Alex's reframe: the scrum is CORRECT Blood Bowl; humans resolve it by BLOCKING markers off the ball before scooping — and v1 was pacifist BY DESIGN (k=0), removing the exact tool that resolves its own equilibrium. Also: 17 gfi/ep under bc_coef 1.0 proves the potentials behaviorally out-shout a full-strength anchor. Premortem of v2 caught a second flaw before launch: ball_gain 0.3 vs loss -0.2 breaks the |loss|>gain anti-farming invariant (pickup-drop laundering, team-level possession pays re-scoops) → v2 ships 0.3/-0.4. BALLHAWK-V2 = scrum-literate: fetch 0.05, carry 0.2, gain 0.3/loss -0.4, k-knobs at HALF (blocking the scrum becomes +EV) — converging back toward synthesis+C with the ball channel amplified and farming-proofed. Expected failure mode (premortem, ~60%): the carry-phase wall — straight-line carrier rushes into a mirror defense that co-evolves; its cure is ASYMMETRIC training (offense vs frozen defense), torch-side freeze support to be built in parallel. Also: 766K SPS on the 64-core/3.4GHz box (7x box-2) — cores_effective x clock is the fleet filter henceforth.
**D43 — The possession annuity (Alex's reward-chain redesign) + the from-kickoff zero.** Probe result that forced it: kzero@1.7B, from-kickoff-only, masked — pickup_attempts 0.000 (the bc prior attempts 0.36-1.0; PPO trained the FREE kickoff scoop away), possession_rate 0.052 (≈ touchbacks), full games of blocking around an untouched ball. Mechanism: the critic prices the possession FUTURE — under mirror defense, pickup (+0.1 once) → targeted → stripped/sacked (loss -0.2, injury -0.15, turnover) nets negative every time; refusing the free ball is the rational policy under lump-sum+fine pricing. Alex's chain audit exposed the inversion: possession was priced as a coupon with an exit fine when it IS the game's income stream. NEW KNOB reward_possession: ending your own team turn holding pays +p/-p ZERO-SUM at the turn boundary (implementation: the possession_rate detector). Funds the whole chain with one knob: want-the-ball (stream entry), protect-the-carrier (protect income), defense bleeds until takeaway; ball_loss fine DELETED in annuity configs (loss = lost stream + opponent's gain — no double fine); 16 binary events/side/game = unfarmable; known trade: mildly rewards stalling (real Blood Bowl). POSSESSION-SPINE ARM live on ex-kzero box: possession 0.03, gain 0.05, loss 0, fetch 0.05/carry 0.2, k-half, anchor 1.0. The kzero-1.8B no-shaping result stands recorded: B-knob fines alone reproduce ball-avoidance.
**D44 — Asymmetric training shipped: the frozen-defense arm is live.** torch trainer grew frozen_enemy_path (training/torch_pufferl_bcreg.patch): non-learner rows play a frozen policy (deepcopy + state_dict, no grad, masked sampling, own LSTM state), learner alternates home/away by env parity, PPO slices to learner rows only (ratio/prio/batch math on train_rows). Deployed as PROFILE-POSS-ASYM on the 64-core box (647K SPS, learner 2048/4096 rows): the full possession-annuity config (D43) vs FROZEN bc_v3b defense — the first run where the learner's offense faces a defense that cannot co-evolve. Rationale chain: D39 (no win progress symmetric) → D43 (possession futures net-negative under mirror play) → premortem (carry-phase wall ~60%) → this. Sister arms: possession-symmetric (control for the asymmetry variable), anneal-s3, ballhawk2 retained at 10B as the scrum-literate reference. Spectator gained the color-coded event-feed sidebar (bbe_feed_hook, POD-only cross-thread per the memorial doctrine) — pickups/blocks/dodges/passes/TDs streaming live.
**D45 — Asym 10B verdict: behavioral divergence WITHOUT win conversion; the prior is the bottleneck.** poss-asym (annuity config vs FROZEN bc_v3b, 647K SPS, 10B in ~4.5h): EIGHT consecutive nonzero tds ticks (0.004-0.018 band) and pickup_success up to 0.14-0.22 while the symmetric twin held absolute zero tds with possession decaying — the asymmetry effect is real and directional. BUT the arbitration tournament (4096 games vs its own frozen opponent, both bias-drop-converted): 97.1% draws, decisive 48.5/51.5 — after 10B steps of practice against a defense that NEVER ADAPTS, the learner cannot beat it. Synthesis of the week's evidence (D35 capacity, D39/D43 possession poison, this): the binding constraint is THE PRIOR — a 0.40-exact iid imitation is a bad Blood Bowl player; the anchor (bc_acc pinned at its 0.396 ceiling throughout) holds the policy at that level; and PPO cannot discover multi-step drives from there even unopposed-by-adaptation. Levers, ranked: (1) anchor RELEASE — bc_coef_floor now configurable (was hard-coded 0.1); ASYM-RELEASE launched overnight from the asym-10B checkpoint with floor 0 (does the policy outgrow its teacher when allowed to leave the human manifold vs a static defense?); (2) sequence-context bc_v4 (the D35 lever — iid zero-state BC is the known ceiling); (3) bigger policy. Tournament caveat noted: CUDA bias-drop conversion applied to both sides equally.
**D46 — Discovery-vs-artifact doctrine (Alex, 2026-06-07): do not patch out inhuman behaviors by aesthetics.** RL's value is uncovering inhuman-but-optimal play (TD-Gammon's doubles, AlphaStar's worker saturation); "looks absurd" is not a valid filter. Discriminator before patching any weird behavior: (1) does it survive GROUNDING — persist when wins/TDs against a competent opponent are the binding currency, not shaped income? (2) is its profit causally routed THROUGH the objective or around it? (3) human rates are evidence, not law. Case study, GFI-spam (~17/ep vs human ~2-5): currently routed AROUND the objective (farms potential income while degrading drives; failed GFIs priced ~zero because under scoring scarcity the opponent can't convert turnovers) — so PRESUMED artifact, but the verdict belongs to the tournament, not taste. Consequences: reward_rush_cost is ANTI-DEGENERACY SCAFFOLDING (k-knob category, to be annealed away once the economy works), never a permanent value statement; deploy taxed-vs-untaxed as an A/B; if the untaxed twin keeps high GFI AND wins, absurd is correct and the tax dies.
**D46-addendum (Alex, 03:32): the real GFI price is positional, and that unifies the disease.** GFIs are individually high-success (5/6); IRL the binding cost is TZ-coverage preservation — a prone player projects no tackle zones, so you GFI only when the squares net something AND that player being down is acceptable. Standing presence is defensive currency (constrains opponent ball movement); under scoring scarcity defense has nothing to defend, so the agent CORRECTLY prices prone-ness at ~zero — GFI-spam is accurate pricing of a worthless asset, not ignorance. Unifies ball-avoidance, scrum-hovering, and GFI-spam as ONE disease: positional value is denominated in points and there are no points. Flat rush tax therefore doubly a crutch (true GFI price is context-dependent: last screener vs idle player); cure remains a working scoring economy. GFI gradient observed across arms: anneal 8.5 → possession 14 → asym-10B 29.7/ep — rushing scales with optimization depth in the broken economy, not with winning (artifact signature per the D46 discriminator).
**D46-addendum-2 (Alex, 03:33): standing presence is protection currency on BOTH sides of the ball** — TZs constrain opponent runners (defense) AND screen your own carrier from a straight rush (offense); a prone screener is an open lane to your ball. Corollary: the annuity arms already mint the OFFENSIVE half (standing screeners protect the +p/turn stream), the defensive half stays unpriced until opponent scoring exists. Testable prediction: GFI discipline should emerge FIRST on the carrying team (sober cage, reckless others) — watch the event ticker / per-team gfi splits.
**D47 — Anchor release verdict: NO breakout, NO collapse — the anchor was never the binding constraint.** asym-release2 (from asym-10B ckpt, frozen bc_v3b defense, bc_coef 0.5 -> 0.000 corrected cosine, capped ~6.03B continuation; stop-condition overshoot noted: runner global_step advances train-batch-width under asymmetry — patch with epoch-based stop or full-width accounting): bc_acc HELD ~0.39-0.42 throughout including ~1.3B steps at bc_coef<0.1 (no manifold drift — PPO updates too local to leave the basin), tds band unchanged (0.004-0.018), gfi ~30/ep unchanged. Tournament 4096 games vs frozen bc_v3b: 96.8% draws, decisive 48.4/51.6 — IDENTICAL to the anchored result (97.1%, 48.5/51.5). D45's anchor-over-binding hypothesis REFUTED: with the leash fully off, against a defense that cannot adapt, PPO still cannot find multi-step scoring play from this prior at this capacity. Remaining levers, now cleanly ranked: (1) BACKPLAY CURRICULUM — filter the demo bank for carrier-near-endzone states so the policy EXPERIENCES scoring densely, expand backward (the bank was literally built for this pattern; cheapest lever, untested); (2) bc_v4 sequence-context prior (D35); (3) bigger policy. The asym infrastructure + annuity economy remain the training architecture; they removed every confound that used to hide this conclusion.
**D48 — BACKPLAY WORKS: first sustained scoring growth in project history.** Stage 1 (demo 0.9, maxdist 6, frozen bc_v3b defense, annuity economy, from bc_v3b): tds 0.045 -> 0.094 -> 0.152 over 2.3B (three rising ticks; every prior run flat ≤0.018), score_diff nonzero and growing (decisive games exist in training at last), and gfi_attempts FALLING (28.8 -> 25.6) as touchdowns become real — the D46 grounding test starting to bite exactly as predicted (recklessness costs points now). Mechanism confirmed: the TD gradient never had mass; placing carriers ≤6 squares from the endzone (90% of starts) gives PPO dense scoring experience to amplify. Stage plan: hold stage 1 until tds plateaus, then maxdist 12, then uniform bank, then kickoff starts — watching for retention at each backward expansion (the Backplay literature's failure mode is forgetting the endgame as the start recedes). Possession-symmetric twin flickered its first nonzero (0.005 @ 8.9B, footnote).
**D49 — The backplay program: three-arm controlled experiment from one checkpoint.** Anneal chain closed (s1-s4, full->zero k, tds 0.000 throughout: exposure-anneal alone never scores) and possession-symmetric capped at 10.1B scoreless (the annuity alone, mirror play: rational ball-avoidance persisted) — both boxes reassigned. ALL THREE FLEET ARMS now branch from the SAME backplay-s1 checkpoint (5.24B, tds ~0.29 rising): bp_s1 flagship (ballhawk box, maxdist 6, untaxed — how far does stage 1 climb), bp_s2 preview (possession box, maxdist 12 — does skill survive backward expansion, parallel instead of serial staging), bp_tax twin (box-2, maxdist 6 + rush_cost 0.015 — the D46 A/B: does pricing GFIs help or does the grounding effect alone suffice). Tier-distribution exports (2d:2d-red) live on all three after fixing a stale binding.c on the flagship box (header synced, binding didn't — partial-sync footgun; counters existed but were never exported). Sweep tracks tds/gfi/2d/2dred per arm.
**D50 — Mid-curriculum tournament calibration: training-tds does not equal winning until starts reach kickoff.** backplay-s1 @ ~7B (training tds ~0.29 from maxdist-6 starts) vs frozen bc_v3b, 4096 full games from kickoff: 96.4% draws, 48.2/51.8 — statistically the predecessors' result (whisper: decisive 119->147, draws 97.1->96.4, not claimable). Mechanism, plainly: the policy converts near-endzone STARTS; full games never reach near-endzone positions because early/mid-game play is unchanged — the endgame skill exists but is unreachable from kickoff. This is the expected mid-curriculum state, not refutation: the backward expansion (s2 maxdist 12 -> uniform -> kickoff) is precisely the machinery meant to connect the opening whistle to the learned endgame. RULE: grounded win-rate arbitration is the graduation exam for the FINAL curriculum stage; per-stage progress is measured by tds-at-stage-starts + retention probes of earlier stages.
**D51 — Curriculum step-size finding: 6->12 overshot, stepping to 9; tax twin OUTSCORING untaxed.** bp_s2 (maxdist 12 from the s1 ckpt): tds flat 0.03-0.07 through 2.1B, no slope (flagship at same depth: 0.15 rising) — 12-square starts demand open-field traversal the policy lacks; known scoring states too rarely reached to bootstrap. Backward expansion needs SMALL steps: relaunched as s2b maxdist 9, same shared checkpoint. Meanwhile bp_tax @1.2B hit tds 0.285-0.349 with gfi ~25-26 — matching/exceeding the flagship's per-step pace WITH fewer rushes: early D46 A/B read says the rush tax costs nothing and may help (cleaner positional play -> better conversion). Flagship grinding 0.30-0.37 @12.7B, slope shallow but alive.
**D52 — Stage 1 closed at tds 0.380 (8x pre-backplay best); s2-DEEP launched (stage-depth experiment).** bp_s1 capped at 15.0B (asymmetric stop overshoot — known): tds ground 0.29 -> 0.380 over the resumed leg, gfi easing 28 -> 27. Tax twin at 1.6B: tds 0.303-0.311, gfi down to 23.0 — still matching the untaxed lineage's pace with ~4 fewer rushes/ep; D46 A/B continues to lean pro-tax.
**D53 — bc_v4: val exact 0.508 (bc_v3b: 0.371, +37% relative) — the obs-v4 information-parity prediction CONFIRMED.** 60K cosine steps, 2,085,330 v4 pairs from 12,304 replays (corpus doubled since bc_v3), by-replay split (1.67M/413K). Heads: type 0.949 / arg 0.840 / sq 0.668. Two factors deliberately confounded (more data + probability planes) — the spec's claim was only that the COMBINATION beats 0.371, which it does decisively; if the decomposition ever matters, train a v3-obs anchor on the same 12K corpus. Consequence: the "0.40-exact prior is a bad Blood Bowl player" ceiling (D45/D47) just moved — a 0.51-exact prior plays meaningfully closer to its teachers, and the whole curriculum program restarts from a stronger base. Next: first obs-v4 arm = bc_v4 anchor + backplay stage-1 knobs + frozen bc_v4 enemy + annuity economy, on the first box that frees.
**D54 — FIRST SIGHTED ARM LIVE: profile-v4-backplay.** s2-deep capped at 15.0B (stage-2-deep band ~0.20-0.22 — converged faster than s2b but to a similar level so far; the depth question stays open in the v3 lineage while v4 supersedes). Final checkpoint 0000014942470144.bin on the stopped disk. **D56 — Sighted stage-1 tournament: 98.8% draws (49.5/50.5) — the D50 rule holds; curriculum position, not prior quality, gates the kickoff exam.** v4_s1_final (15B, tds 0.42-0.49 from maxdist-6 starts) vs bc_v4, 4096 games from kickoff: no conversion — endgame skill remains unreachable from the opening; early-game play is still prior-shaped. **D57 — THE 4x LEVER FIRES: native anchor-free asymmetric training at 2.1M SPS.** profile-v4-native-asym on box-1 (24c judge box!): native CUDA backend, NO bc aux (D47 license), frozen bc_v4 pinned as the selfplay-pool teacher (1-seed league_preseed pool, swap_winrate 1.1 = unreachable, opp_timeout 100B = never; frozen_bank_pct 0.48 — the apb/2 cap means ~48% of envs are vs-teacher, the rest mirror: an accidental but reasonable hybrid), learner warm from v4_s1_final_cuda, same annuity+backplay-s2 env knobs. SPS 2.1M vs torch twins' 0.6-0.77M — 3x on the WEAKEST box; the 64c boxes should exceed it. Early tds 0.229@0.5B sits in the stage-2 band = anchor-free learning parity plausible; the real test is the curve vs the torch flagship at matched steps over the next hours. If parity holds, the program's step budget just tripled at constant cost and the torch backend retires to bc_vN training only.
**D58 — THE 4x LEVER SHIPS: native anchor-free architecture verified at parity, 3.42x throughput.** parity_report.py (tools/, new) on the live A/B at matched steps to 5B: SPS 2.10M (native) vs 0.61M (torch) = 3.42x ON THE WEAKEST BOX (24c); tds PARITY (native 0.318 vs torch 0.355 at 5B, -10.4% within band, native slope STEEPER 0.080 vs 0.049/B — anchor-free learning holds, confirming D47's release-is-safe license at production scale); wall-clock-to-0.45-tds native ~13min vs torch ~23min (native needs more STEPS but far less TIME). Anchor-free training is correct AND ~3.4x cheaper per unit progress. SHIPPED: tools/run_native_asym.sh (TEACHER/WARM/STEPS contract, pinning knobs hardcoded + snapshot_interval 1e12 to suppress the ~600MB/hr pool pollution the audit caught, off-box refusal, LIVE check), tools/parity_report.py (the verdict harness), fleet-ops skill "Native anchor-free architecture" section (native=all RL stages, torch=bc_vN+aux-research ONLY; one backend per box — --float and native artifacts are mutually exclusive). 9-agent ultracode audit verdicts SOUND/ISSUES/SOUND; teacher provably immutable (every selfplay rotation trigger unsatisfiable at swap_winrate 1.1 / opp_timeout 1e11). OPEN/CONFOUNDED: block_2dred_frac native 0.116 vs torch 0.171 (-32%) — both warm-started from v4_s1_final ~0.20, so native TRAINS THE RED-DICE HABIT AWAY where torch holds it; HYPOTHESIS (the bc anchor pulls block selection back toward the noisy human prior; without it PPO+planes rationalize faster) is confounded with the opponent mechanism (pool vs frozen-enemy-path) — isolate before claiming (torch-no-anchor or native-small-aux arm). Box-1's installed build predates the SPS pass (55b43f3): live run is correct but pre-optimization; a future native rebuild picks up both — documented, do NOT rebuild mid-run.
**D59 — Hyperthreading/thread-pool answer: we were NOT using the cores optimally on quota-limited boxes; fixed +4.4x.** Alex's question, investigated empirically: the possession-tax box read 114K SPS vs the IDENTICAL-config flagship's 592K. Root cause (measured, not theorized): `nproc` reports VISIBLE logical CPUs, but vast.ai containers cap CPU TIME via cgroup CFS quota. possession box: nproc=255 (128 physical x2 HT) but cfs_quota_us 6120000/100000 = 61 CPUs allowed. With OMP_NUM_THREADS unset, PyTorch + OpenBLAS auto-size their intra-op pools to nproc=255, so the trainer ran 641 threads thrashing on 61 CPUs of real time. ballhawk: nproc=64 ~ quota 61, only 162 threads, mild 2.7x oversub, fine. FIX: cap OMP/OPENBLAS/MKL/NUMEXPR_NUM_THREADS to the detected cgroup quota (v1 cpu.cfs_quota_us AND v2 cpu.max, clamped <= nproc) at launch — baked into tools/run_synthesis_c.sh + tools/run_native_asym.sh. The env-stepping OMP is INDEPENDENT (vec num_threads=20, explicit pragma) — this only tames the math-library pools. MEASURED on tax twin relaunch: 641->186 threads, 114K->~500K SPS (4.4x), now matching the flagship. The env step's own HT usage (loadavg 64 on 64 threads) is fine; physical-only vs HT for env stepping is the remaining Tier-4 A/B (lower priority). Flagship left undisturbed mid-A/B (it picks up the cap at stage-3 relaunch). NOTE: native backend (box-1) was already optimal (nproc=24=quota, GPU-bound).
**D60 — The native arm's low 2d-red is REAL and PERSISTENT but stays CONFOUNDED — do not promote to "anchor suppresses rationality."** block_2dred_frac on profile-v4-native-asym held 0.106-0.109 across the whole run to 9.4B (5+ consecutive stable ticks), vs torch v4 arms 0.17-0.20 — both lineages warm-started from v4_s1_final (~0.20), so the native config actively TRAINS THE RED-DICE HABIT DOWN where torch holds it. Tempting headline ("the bc anchor was pulling block selection back toward the noisy human prior"), but the native arm differs from torch in TWO ways simultaneously: (a) NO bc aux loss, (b) opponent = selfplay pool vs torch's frozen-enemy-path. Per D46 discipline this is NOT a clean finding. ISOLATION EXPERIMENT to settle it (queued, not urgent): a torch arm with bc_coef 0 (anchor off, same frozen-enemy-path) — if ITS 2dred also falls to ~0.11, the anchor is the cause; if it stays ~0.18, the opponent mechanism is. Until then: persistent phenomenon, cause unattributed. (Other scheduled-check reconciliation: SPS diagnosis -> D59 fix, tds parity -> D58, v3_tax left as legacy straggler/box-2 repurpose candidate, native caps ~15:30, balance $91.50.)
**D61 — Human baseline MEASURED (12,722 games, 453,617 team-turns) — corrects guessed priors, especially GFI.** Per-game / per-team-turn rates from the FUMBBL corpus: blockRoll 88.8/game (2.49/turn — Blood Bowl is constant violence, high contact is NORMAL not pathological), dodgeRoll 25.7/game (0.72/turn), **goForItRoll 17.4/game (0.49/turn)**, pickUpRoll 7.3/game (0.21/turn), passRoll 2.0/game, foul 2.9/game, pickup_success 0.670, block tiers 77.5% 2d / 1.7% 2dred / 8.5% 3d / 12.4% 1d. KEY CORRECTION: the D46/D52 "gfi artifact" narrative assumed humans GFI ~2-5/game; the TRUE figure is ~17/game (once per ~2 team-turns). Our agents' GFI rate is therefore much closer to human than the artifact framing claimed — the rush tax may be solving a smaller problem than thought, and per-team-turn (not per-curriculum-episode) is the only valid agent-vs-human GFI comparison. DELIVERED: tools/game_stats.py (agent dashboard vs docs/human-baseline.json, marks toward-human / PAST-human / context per metric — human is a plausibly-optimal REFERENCE, not a ceiling; superhuman SHOULD diverge on context axes) + tools/eval_game_stats.sh (full-game-from-kickoff frozen measurement, the ONLY human-comparable mode; training dashboards use curriculum starts and are NOT comparable). Methodology note: human is plausibly-optimal, not optimal — a superhuman policy may legitimately throw fewer/better blocks, hold the ball more, GFI less.
**D62 — Native stage-2 capped at 30B; stage-3 (maxdist 12) launched. Native arch verdict reaffirmed.** profile-v4-native-asym final (30B, anchor-free, frozen bc_v4 teacher, 2.0-2.1M SPS throughout): tds 0.432, block_2dred_frac 0.111 (HALF the torch arms' ~0.17-0.19 — the cleanest block-rationality of any arm, still confounded per D60 but persistent to 30B), possession_rate 0.195 (best recorded, ties the torch flagship), pickup_success 0.275, gfi 22.6. The native arm matched torch on scoring at 3.4x the throughput for the whole run. Stage-3 warm from the 30B ckpt at maxdist 12 (the +3 ladder), TEACHER bc_v4_cuda, 30B. **D66 — D60 confound RESOLVED: the 2dred gap is TWO-FACTOR, opponent/backend mechanism the larger share (~60%), bc anchor the smaller (~40%).** Isolation arm v4-d60-bccoef0 (taiwan, torch --float obs-v4, frozen-enemy bc_v4.bin, bc-coef 0 = single variable vs torch_s3's 1.0, maxdist 12, warm from v4_s2tax 15B): at 10.9B block_2dred_frac settled at mean 0.145 (last-30 band 0.124-0.154). Reference points: torch-with-anchor arms ~0.16-0.18, native anchor-free ~0.108-0.111. Removing ONLY the anchor moved 2dred from ~0.17 to ~0.145 — about 40% of the native-torch gap; the remaining ~60% comes from the opponent/backend mechanism (selfplay-pool teacher mix vs head-on frozen-enemy, plus any bf16-vs-fp32 effect — these two remain bundled; a further isolation would be a native arm with head-on frozen enemy, LOW priority). Neither early hypothesis was right alone: "the anchor pulls block selection toward the noisy human prior" is TRUE but explains a minority; who-you-practice-against shapes block-dice taste MORE than the imitation pull does. Arm stopped at verdict (served its purpose); taiwan box stopped to conserve (nothing unique on it: big bank now on Mac+possession+japan, bc_v4 anchors on japan+ballhawk). Healthy side-note: the arm's tds 0.369 at 10.9B with bc-coef 0 confirms anchor-free torch trains fine — the anchor is not load-bearing for learning, consistent with D62's native verdict.
**D67 — Pickup curriculum stages 1-2 FAILED TRANSFER: drill-locked skill + catastrophic forgetting of game play. Drill doctrine amended: drills need a scrimmage mix.** From-kickoff eval of pickup-s2 final (15B maxdist-2 + 15B maxdist-4, demo-reset-pct 0.9) vs its ancestor v4_s2tax, BOTH run through identical bias-stripping round-trips (control proved stripping harmless: ancestor kept its profile — pickup_attempts 0.714, success 0.429, dodges 13.0, gfi 11.9): pickup-s2 from kickoff = pickup_attempts 0.000, success 0.000, dodges 3.7, gfi 2.7, tds 0.000, blocks 36.8 — REGRESSED on every axis INCLUDING the drilled skill. Within drill episodes the skill exists (~0.6 attempts/ep, ~50% success) but NEVER deploys from kickoff — context-locked. Mechanism: 90% of 30B steps started mid-game at a loose ball; kickoff-phase play (approach, formation, multi-turn drive) atrophied. CONTRAST: the flagship kickoff arm (v4-native-kickoff, zero dedicated pickup drilling, ladder = backplay->uniform->kickoff) scoops 0.532/game in full games — in-context exposure taught the skill the drill could not transfer. DOCTRINE (drills-design.md amended): drills must be MIXED with scrimmage (real practice is ~30% drills / 70% integrated play); demo-reset-pct 0.9 is drill saturation and overwrites game-context behavior; the backplay ladder accidentally respected this by GRADUATING to kickoff, the pickup lineage never mixed back. FIX-TEST LAUNCHED (possession): pickup-s3mix — same maxdist 4, demo-reset-pct 0.5, warm from the SAME ancestor warm blob as pickup-s1 (v4_s2tax_warm_cuda.bin), 15B; readout = from-kickoff table at cap vs ancestor (did 50/50 teach scooping without destroying game play?). This answers the mix-ratio question for ALL future drills (passing, cage-crack) before the drill compiler ships more banks. Also fixed: eval_game_stats.sh abspath footgun (same class as run_synthesis_c ANCHOR); converter --to-torch zero-fills biases by design (native flat = weights-only) — bias-stripping measured harmless on a torch-trained ckpt (control above), so round-trip evals are valid with equal treatment.

**D71 — RTX 2070 baseload rig ONLINE (2026-06-10): native fp32 ~190K SPS, role = evals + patient drill experiments, NOT production.** Onboarded Alex's Windows/RTX-2070 desktop as a free always-on node over Tailscale (wsl-ubuntu 100.97.209.46 / windows-host 100.66.30.28, user rache). WSL2 Ubuntu 25.10, 16 threads, 11GB WSL RAM (host has more; bump via .wslconfig if OOM), 954GB disk, driver 595.79, GPU passthrough via /dev/dxg. Build gotchas (all Linux-WSL specific, NOT on the vast pytorch-docker boxes): (1) Ubuntu 25.10 ships Python 3.14 (no torch wheels) -> built a uv-managed Python 3.11 venv to match the vast cpython-311; (2) needed apt: clang libomp-dev ccache nvidia-cuda-toolkit (nvcc 12.4); pip: pybind11 setuptools numpy via `uv pip install --python .venv/bin/python`; (3) build.sh links -lnccl -lcudnn which the apt toolkit lacks but torch BUNDLES — symlink `.venv/.../nvidia/{nccl,cudnn}/lib/lib{nccl.so.2->.so,cudnn.so.9->.so}` and export LIBRARY_PATH + LD_LIBRARY_PATH to those two dirs for BOTH build and runtime; (4) NVCC_ARCH=sm_75 (Turing); --float build = prec=4 (fp32, correct — Turing has no bf16). SPS: native fp32 (no --slowly) ~190K vs torch --slowly ~115K — native wins here too, USE IT. Per-core ~12K vs vast native's ~91K/core (WSL + consumer-CPU overhead; the plan's 1-2M guess was optimistic by ~10x). Practical: eval (8M steps) ~42s = free evals; 15B drill ~22h = viable overnight; 30B flagship stage ~44h = too slow, flagship stays on vast. Reboot-autostart-recovery test in progress (validates Tailscale+WSL+sshd auto-rejoin before trusting unattended). Next: resident Claude Code + babysitter cron on the box. Full build recipe -> fleet-ops skill / a new docs/2070-rig.md.

**D79 — MODULATION CONFIRMED (directionally): the same checkpoint plays DIFFERENT FOOTBALL by roster.** Pinned-mirror evals of the s2 ckpt vs the D75 per-team human rows: as WOOD ELF — dodges 18.2, blocks 15.3, tds 1.33, pass 0.40; as DWARF — dodges 6.0 (3.0x FEWER, human ratio 12x same direction), blocks 21.2 (1.4x MORE, human 1.8x), tds 0.46 (humans also score less with dwarves: 0.73 vs 1.27), pass 0.39 (flat — passing too nascent to modulate). 2-3 of 3 pre-registered metrics shift toward the matching human row; dodge modulation is dramatic and unmistakable. MECHANISM CAVEAT (honest attribution): modulation flows through the obs — stat lines, skills, and especially the B-plane step-success odds tell the policy dwarves can't dodge — i.e. roster-conditional play is LEARNED ODDS-FOLLOWING, not memorized team identity (there is no team-id input by design). That is the same mechanism human coaches use (dwarves dodge less because it fails); it is genuine adaptive strategy, attributed correctly. Sample-size: 3-15 games/eval, directional. Next-level test someday: asymmetric matchups (elf VS dwarf) + whether it targets the OPPONENT's weaknesses.

**D82 — v5 PATH-ACTIONS built, Codex-reviewed, mechanically verified, BALLOON LAUNCHED (Alex: "LETS FUCKING TRY IT BABY").** Design: ENGINE UNTOUCHED; env-layer knob `macro_moves` — STEP square head selects ANY reachable destination; bbe_macro_reach (O(V²) Dijkstra, cost 1 + 50/dodge + 12/rush, parent pointers, approx P-product for the obs B plane) computed at fill_mask for the deciding MOVE window; mask marks all reachable dests; bbe_decode routes non-adjacent picks via bbe_macro_plan; c_step follows the path while uninterrupted (TEST windows/knockdowns/occupied/activation-end break + clear; policy re-plans after interruptions); per-step bbe_count_action keeps dodge/gfi/pickup metrics + rush tax exact; post-loop accounting is state-diff so possession/TD/knockdowns stay correct. Knob-off = v4 (all code gated). CODEX REVIEW (.codex-reviews/v5-macro-moves.md) found+fixed: HIGH may_move gate missing (plain-BLOCK MOVE frames + post-pickup TTM could take illegal trusted steps → added kind/MV_BLOCK_DONE guard + decode mover-match hardening + obs-B read-only memo), MEDIUM max_decisions overshoot (cap checked in-loop now), LOW reset scratch (cleared in bbe_reset_match); confirmed ego-mirroring/bounds/clamp/interruptions sound. ENGAGEMENT PROVEN by server-side counters: 301K paths planned / 1.0M continuation steps in a 100s random smoke (~4.3 sq/macro) — an earlier 0/1213 test-harness result was an ego-row off-by-one in the TEST, not the code. **D82-HYPOTHESIS (pre-registered, 2026-06-10 17:00, before any balloon data):** Mechanism: the square head is shared across action types (trained spatial priors from pass/kick/block targets) but adjacent-only in MOVE windows — warm adaptation seeds from those priors; macro credit density (whole move per decision) is the learning accelerant. PREDICTIONS: (1) 85%: early tds dip to ~0.3-0.6 within 0.5B (semantic shock — expected, not failure). (2) The crux: 55% tds re-crosses 1.0 by ~8B with steeper slope than v4 kickoff-6 → balloon flies; 30% parity-no-win by 15B → A/B decides; 15% no recovery by 5B → needs bc_v5 destination pairs / fresh square head. (3) Side-prediction: gfi+dodge attempts/game fall 30-50% vs v4 (router only risks when the destination demands — note as confound for human-baseline comparisons). (4) If flying, v5 movement visibly more purposeful on BBTV before metrics confirm. (5) Main pathology risk: PPO instability from 3-4x per-decision return rescale (entropy/value-loss spike in first 1B = the tell; fix is LR/value-coef, not abandonment).

**D89 — possession_rate is CONFOUNDED — do NOT read agent 0.184 vs human 0.47 as a ball-security weakness (Alex correction, 2026-06-10 D46 catch).** Measured human possession_rate = 0.47 (turn-ends holding the ball, 300-game sample; tools/human_possession.py, full-corpus running). Initial (WRONG) read: "agent holds ball <half as often = possession is the next frontier." Alex's correction, which is right: a TOUCHDOWN ends the drive with the scorer NOT holding (ball resets to kickoff), so possession_rate is MECHANICALLY suppressed by scoring efficiency — efficient scorers show LOW possession by construction. Compounded by the OPPONENT confound: agent games (self-vs-self in eval; agent weak on defense) have no real defensive resistance, so drives are SHORT (score-reset-repeat) → few mid-drive holding turn-ends; human-vs-human games have both sides defending, so possession is CONTESTED across many turns before converting/turning over → many holding turn-ends. So human 0.47 vs agent 0.184 reflects drive LENGTH (= defense quality + scoring speed), not ball security. DOCTRINE: possession_rate is only comparable between policies measured against the SAME opponent at the SAME scoring rate; the human figure is from human-vs-human and is NOT a clean agent target. The real ball-security question needs agent-vs-STRONG-opponent (v5 flagship as its own teacher) where drives are contested — at which point possession_rate becomes informative. Leaving possession OUT of the human-comparable target set in game_stats.py (mark context, not higher/lower).
**D90 — THE CONTESTED ERA BEGINS (Alex root-cause + directive, 2026-06-11: "No one is contesting the ball. No one is fighting to stop the opponent from scoring."). Diagnosis: every observed pathology — no defense, uncontested loose balls, aimless defensive movement, suspect record-ladder — traces to the DEAD OPPONENT POOL: since D57 all arms trained vs the frozen bc_v4 teacher (51% clone), which the learner outgrew long ago; defense and ball-denial have had ZERO gradient because the opponent never threatened anything. Four actions fired:**
1. **Possession metric fixed (env + human tool, same definition):** a turn ending in your own TD counts as ending WITH possession (you carried it in). Annuity unchanged (still requires HELD; reward_td pays the score). Pre-D90 possession_rate numbers are NOT comparable to post-D90. Human baseline re-measuring under the new definition (old-definition human = 0.476 over 14,285 games / 1.07M turns).
2. **v5-contested LAUNCHED (ballhawk):** TEACHER = the v5-kickoff 1.625 flagship cap ITSELF (first non-bc_v4 opponent ever), WARM from same, macro on, kickoff-pure, 30B. v5-kickoff2 (gen-3 vs the dead teacher) killed — low marginal value. PRE-REGISTERED: training tds CRASHES initially (real defense exists for the first time); pickup_attempts rise (loose balls contested); defensive behaviors (marking, screening, ball-denial) become visible on BBTV within a generation; from-kickoff eval may dip while defense develops — head-to-head is the honest score.
3. **Head-to-head tournament = the new scoreboard:** training-tds records vs a static teacher are NOT cross-lineage comparable (partly exploitation of a fixed target). v5-kickoff cap vs v4 kickoff-8 cap, 2048 games x TWO env configs (macro on = v5 semantics / macro off = v4 semantics) because the action-space asymmetry handicaps one side per config — bracket the truth. Running on the 2070 (v5-balloon killed — replicate purpose served; rig_relaunch.sh disabled pending new role).
4. **League unpinning = the structural end-state (design):** after v5-contested proves the shape, switch to the existing-but-pinned league machinery (training/selfplay_league.patch, run_league.sh): seeded bank {bc_v4, v4-kickoff8 cap, v5-kickoff cap, + run snapshots}, swap_winrate 0.55 (the ini's intended default), snapshot_interval live — opponent grows with the learner permanently; no more static-target overfitting. The frozen-teacher era (D57→D90) ends deliberately. Non-move (doctrine): NO defensive reward shaping — D67-D69 proved distributions teach and bribes distort; defense needed an opponent, not a bounty.

**D97 — RATCHET SLOPE FLATTENING: gen-3 beats gen-2 only 55% decisive (down from gen-2-over-gen-1's 70%) — diminishing returns confirmed, not yet collapse. Gen-3 finals (30B, teacher=gen-2 cap): tds 1.453, possession 0.223, pickups 2.666 — possession continuing its climb (gen1 ~0.16 -> gen2 0.182 -> gen3 0.223) while pickups continue falling (3.072 -> 2.917 -> 2.666), the efficiency-not-volume signal noted in the trajectory review. Reading: each ratchet generation still wins against its predecessor, but the margin is compressing toward the ~50% the league-vs-ratchet dead heat (D96) already showed at the regime level — consistent with a single S-curve where the ratchet's concentrated self-play pressure saturates faster than the league's diverse pressure. Gen-3 cap backed up to B2 (v4_contested3_cap.bin). Gen-4 launched on japan (TEACHER=WARM=gen-3 cap, stepwise kickoff-pure, 30B, pid 18752) — one more slope sample before any lead-bet call; pre-registration: if gen-4-vs-gen-3 drops to ~50% (true plateau), the league-2 lineage (currently 16.0B/30B, tds climbing 1.26->1.33->1.39, healthy under skill-exposure) becomes the lead bet and the ratchet either retires or gets a perturbation (curriculum widening, fresh opponent diversity). **D97-A — CODEX REVIEW of the H1/H2/H3 pivot (.codex-reviews/growth-plan.md): catches a NUMERIC ERROR in D97 and rewrites the gen-4 decision rule before it fires. The error: D97 read tournament `A=0.550 draw=0.419` as "55% decisive," but `puffer match`'s A/B fields already split draws 50/50 into each side's rate — the correct decisive-rate formula (the one bt_fit.py implements) is `(A - 0.5*draw)/(1-draw)`. Recomputed: D97 (gen3-vs-gen2) = 58.6% decisive, not 55%. D95 (gen2-vs-gen1, A=0.631 draw=0.337) = 69.8% (matches the "70%" claim — that one was read correctly). D96 (dead heat, A=0.505 draw=0.418) = 50.9% (also correct). REVISED slope: 69.8% -> 58.6%, an 11.2pt drop — still meaningful deceleration, but 58.6% is NOT "near the 50% plateau" as D97 implied; the "near-plateau" framing was an overcall. REVISED gen-4 decision rule (replaces D97's 50%/60% thresholds), defined on decisive-rate-after-draw-conversion (printed-A equivalents at draw~0.42: 50%dec~=0.500A, 53%dec~=0.514A, 60%dec~=0.558A): <=53% decisive AND H1 ladder shows gen4 not clearly above gen3/league2 -> retire clean ratchet, both boxes to H2/H3. >=60% decisive with CI clear of 55% -> keep one ratchet slot (gen-5). 53-60% decisive (a range that NOW INCLUDES gen3's own 58.6%) -> "slowing but alive," do not retire on this tournament alone; corroborate via H1 ladder + league2-vs-gen3 before deciding. STRUCTURAL fixes adopted: (1) H2 pool capped at <=8 frozen banks (selfplay.py hard RuntimeError above 8; frozen_bank_pct must drop to ~0.06 for 8 banks vs 0.08 for 5 to stay under the apb/2 cap) — curated composition (one weak anchor, one kickoff-era specialist, one v5/macro artifact, one older ratchet, one latest ratchet, one league cap, one skill-exposure cap if league-2 passes, one H3-exploiter slot), NOT literal "every cap ever made." (2) H3 gets staged 5B/10B/15B go/no-go reads (not a single 15B verdict), warm-start preference league2 > league1 > v5-contested (favor a real contender over stylistic-purity-only). (3) bt_fit.py being enhanced (bg, .codex-impl/btfit-enhance-run-*.md) with Wilson 95% CIs, a score-based (non-draw-stripped) Elo table alongside decisive-only, and a full pairwise residual table to catch non-transitivity before crowning a single H1 champion — use a TOP CLUSTER for warm-start selection unless the gap is clearly outside noise. Ladder (21 pairings) running on 2070, 13/21 done.**
**D98 — H1 ANCHORED LADDER RESULTS + a major methodological finding: single 2048-game tournaments can swing ~95 Elo between identical re-runs, larger than the entire top-cluster spread. Round-robin of 7 lineage caps (bc_v4, kickoff8, v5contested, gen1-3, league1; 21 pairings, 2048 games each, stepwise/macro=0; ~1200-1600 decisive games/pairing) fit via tools/bt_fit.py (anchor=bc_v4=0 Elo, scale 400):

DECISIVE-Elo ranking: gen2 4930.0 > gen3 4883.7 ~= league1 4882.7 (1.0 apart) > gen1 4803.0 (-80 from cluster) > kickoff8 4685.8 (-117) > v5contested 4435.8 (-250) > bc_v4 0.0 (effectively dead: raw_strength 1e-12, loses 100% of decisive games to ALL SIX other anchors, including v5contested).
SCORE-BASED (draws=0.5) ranking AGREES on ordering except gen3/league1 swap (league1 282.2 > gen3 274.4, 7.8 Elo apart) -- the two metrics corroborate each other everywhere except inside the noise-dominated top cluster.

TOP CLUSTER {gen2, gen3, league1} spans only 47.3 Elo and is statistically INDISTINGUISHABLE at this sample size -- the two largest residuals in the full pairwise table are gen2-vs-league1 (fit 0.568 vs empirical 0.508, |err| 0.059) and gen3-vs-league1 (fit 0.501 vs empirical 0.554, |err| 0.053), i.e. the noisiest pairings are exactly the ones INSIDE this cluster.

THE HEADLINE FINDING: this ladder's gen2-vs-gen3 pairing (A=gen2 0.530, draw=0.404 -> gen2 decisive 55.0%, 95% CI [52.3%,57.8%]) DIRECTLY CONTRADICTS D97's gen3-vs-gen2 tournament from ~1 hour earlier on the SAME checkpoints, SAME config (A=gen3 0.550, draw=0.419 -> gen3 decisive 58.6%). Converting both to Elo: D97 said gen3 +60.3 over gen2; this ladder says gen2 +34.9 over gen3 -- a ~95 Elo swing on nominally the same measurement, and D97's 58.6% falls FAR outside this ladder's [52.3%,57.8%] CI for the reverse direction. 95 Elo exceeds the ENTIRE top-cluster's 47.3 Elo span. CONCLUSION: a single 2048-game `puffer match` has MUCH larger true variance than the naive per-pairing Wilson CI suggests (the CI assumes i.i.d. Bernoulli over ~1200 "decisive games" but the effective independent sample size is evidently far smaller -- likely correlated outcomes within a run, e.g. shared procgen/seed structure across the env batch). NO SINGLE TOURNAMENT, including the queued gen4-vs-gen3 and league2-vs-gen3, can be decision-grade alone for anything inside a ~100-Elo band.

PROTOCOL AMENDMENT (supersedes D97-A's single-tournament gray-zone language): when gen-4 and league-2 cap, do NOT rely on one gen4-vs-gen3 / league2-vs-gen3 pairing for the retire/keep call. Instead EXTEND THE LADDER -- add each new cap via EXTRA_ANCHORS and run it against all existing anchors (7-8 new pairings each, reuse --resume). A cap's fitted Elo from ~8000+ decisive games across 7-8 opponents averages out single-pairing noise far better than one pairing's ~1200 games. Decision becomes: does the new cap's fitted Elo clearly exceed the {gen2,gen3,league1} cluster (by visibly more than the cluster's own ~50 Elo internal spread, with the full-ladder CIs as support), land WITHIN the cluster (= "still in the pack," itself meaningful for the retire/keep call per D97-A's spirit), or fall below it? Single pairwise tournaments remain useful as quick informal reads but are demoted to non-decisive.

OTHER FINDINGS: bc_v4 is now a "free win" for everything (confirms H4/bc_v5-refresh motivation -- it's a fine pool FLOOR but contributes zero gradient as a "contender"). v5-contested confirms its D93 retirement (clearly weakest non-dead anchor). gen1 sits clearly (~80-127 Elo) below the {gen2,gen3,league1} cluster -- the contested-era ratchet DID produce a real, ladder-visible jump from gen1 to {gen2,gen3}, even though gen2-vs-gen3's internal order is noise. Raw output: /tmp/anchored_ladder.csv + bt_fit.py on the 2070.**

NUMERICAL NOTE: bc_v4-anchored absolute Elo values are NOT stable across ladder extensions (gen2 was 4930.0 in D98's 7-node fit, 1755.2 in this 8-node fit -- bc_v4 has zero decisive wins against anyone, so its raw_strength floor value is renormalization-dependent and swings the WHOLE anchored scale by ~3000 Elo between fits). RELATIVE spacings among non-degenerate nodes are roughly stable (gen3/league1 gaps from gen2: -46/-47 in D98 vs -27/-38 here) and are what matter for cluster-membership calls; absolute Elo numbers should not be quoted cross-fit. Future ladder anchor should be a node with a healthy win/loss mix (e.g. gen1 or kickoff8), not bc_v4, if absolute stability across extensions is needed.

(2) pkill -f '[p]uffer train' inside a heredoc/bash -c whose OWN command line contains the literal string "puffer train" (e.g. the nohup launch line later in the same script) will self-match and kill the launcher before it starts -- ALWAYS run the kill as a SEPARATE ssh invocation from the launch script.
