**D187 — THE FROZEN 6B R0 CURVE IMPROVES AGAINST ITS STATIC TRAINING POOL BUT CANNOT SELECT A CHECKPOINT; IT EXPOSES ACTION-COVERAGE AND REWARD-ATTRIBUTION GAPS (2026-07-14).** An append-only seed-42 prefix through exact step `6,005,587,968` contains 45,815 independent schema-2 train panels and 4,821,395 full-kickoff episodes, file SHA-256 `7fa83012f4bc9f0beb5a74d3cf7c3ea8618b93259d339ae865ee3f9246c17b5f`; every clip, non-finite, engine-error, demo, and fallback total is zero. First-versus-last 500M windows move frozen-bank-episode-weighted static-pool score `0.53378 -> 0.62083`; all-episode-weighted illegal/sampled-repair fraction moves `0.21612 -> 0.17980`, blocks versus the carrier `1.1687 -> 2.0863`, and carrier-target fraction `0.08655 -> 0.17509`, while blocks thrown fall `14.4928 -> 12.7380`. The risk mix is not simply more conservative: 1D rises `0.18102 -> 0.20638` and 2D-red rises `0.03877 -> 0.04433` as carrier targeting doubles. Rush intentions rise `17.3866 -> 20.1724` despite the one-sided `0.015` tax, an average `0.3026` match-wide charge in the last window. Pass intentions fall `0.02132 -> 0.01473` per game and handoffs remain about `0.00016`; exact-BB2025 human references are `1.99344` passes and `1.18705` handoffs per game, but those are plausibility canaries, never reward targets. Touchdowns, ball progress, and half-billion static-pool scores are non-monotonic, and the static banks are in-pool training opponents. DECISION: no live panel, BBTV game, human-stat distance, or newest checkpoint may select or promote R0. Post-run characterization must use the predeclared 0/1/2/4/6/8/10/12B paired matrix in `docs/plans/r0-milestone-evaluation.md`, common match seeds, both native roles, raw seed strata, and the exact cluster bootstrap; learned anchors remain lineage-connected transfer, not independent holdout. For future reward work, prioritize a matched gamma-corrected distance-PBRS/anneal study, the already-declared no-rush ablation, and replay-derived pass/handoff scenarios rather than paying action imitation. Before claiming which shaping term dominates, add per-component emitted-reward attribution: current telemetry proves total integrity and event counts but cannot decompose distance, possession, block-EV, sequencing, and Rush contributions. This finding does not amend the live D185/D186 queues or authorize any production change.

**D188 — CORRECTION: D187 MIXED ENDPOINT MASKS AND OMITTED PANEL EPISODE WEIGHTS FROM STATIC-POOL SCORE; ITS QUALITATIVE VERDICT STANDS (2026-07-14).** Puffer normalizes every environment field by each dashboard panel's completed-episode count `n`, including both `hist_score_bank_*` and `hist_n_bank_*`. Static-pool score must therefore be `sum(hist_score_bank_i * n) / sum(hist_n_bank_i * n)`, while ordinary fields are `sum(metric * n) / sum(n)`. Reanalysis of the same immutable 45,815-panel, 4,821,395-episode prefix, SHA-256 `7fa83012f4bc9f0beb5a74d3cf7c3ea8618b93259d339ae865ee3f9246c17b5f`, also found that D187's scratch table mixed nominal-6B and checkpoint-overshoot endpoint masks across columns. One reproducible `(0, 0.5B]` versus `(5.5B, 6.0B]` table gives static-pool score `0.5337228569 -> 0.6205900025`; illegal fraction `0.21612097 -> 0.17980461`; blocks versus carrier `1.16865555 -> 2.08632319`; carrier-target fraction `0.08654711 -> 0.17529117`; blocks thrown `14.49276152 -> 12.73802963`; 1D fraction `0.18101643 -> 0.20656826`; 2D-red fraction `0.03877255 -> 0.04434671`; Rush intentions `17.38658696 -> 20.16038781`; pass intentions `0.02131751 -> 0.01469562`; and handoffs `0.00010667 -> 0.00016432`. The first band contains 3,810 panels, 365,615 episodes, 175,000.000869 frozen-bank games, and score sum 93,401.500416; the last has 3,815 panels, 395,560 episodes, 183,050.000779 games, and score sum 113,599.000447. Every integrity total remains zero. The exact source ends at `6,005,587,968`, but its 5.59M-step overshoot is excluded from the nominal endpoint band. These corrections are small and preserve D187's carrier-focus/risk/action-coverage directions, in-pool/non-monotonic caveat, no-selection verdict, fixed post-run milestone protocol, and future research priorities. DECISION: cite D188's unified values wherever D187's endpoint numbers are used; preserve D187 append-only, and require source hashes, explicit interval boundaries, panel-episode weighting, and unequal-panel-size regression coverage in any reusable curve analyzer. This correction does not amend either live vacation queue or authorize any production change.

**D189 — BBTV'S GPU-BUILT MATCH SERVER WOULD STRAND THE PINNED VACATION OVERFLOW; MOVE ONLY THE VIEWER TO A PROVEN CPU BUILD (2026-07-14).** The primary/overflow autonomy review initially inferred that BBTV could not block the handoff because checkpoint conversion sets `CUDA_VISIBLE_DEVICES=""`. Live inspection falsified that inference: the exact parser pinned in `PRIMARY_COMPLETION_CONFIG.json` returned trainer PID `431596` and current BBTV match-server PID `459307`, and repeated `nvidia-smi` samples plus `/proc/<pid>/fd` showed the viewer holding `/dev/dxg`. `follow_latest.py` isolated only conversion; the server child inherited GPU visibility. This is terminal for utilization if left unchanged because both the primary completion report and the overflow starter's immediate recheck require an empty compute-PID list. A spare-port probe established a second constraint: hiding CUDA removed the probe PID from the parser, but the current viewer has `pufferlib._C.gpu=1`, so PuffeRL failed with `RuntimeError: No CUDA GPUs are available` while moving the policy. DECISION: neither queue, its pins, nor its gates may be weakened. Build a separate fp32 CPU Blood Bowl viewer in `/home/rache/bloodbowl-rl-bbtv-cpu/vendor/PufferLib` with `./build.sh bloodbowl --cpu`; require the launcher to prove that the imported `_C` resides in that tree and reports `env_name=bloodbowl`, `gpu=0`, and `precision_bytes=4`; hide CUDA from each match child; and before switching only `bbstream`, require a real spare-port `hello`/`match_start`/`snapshot` cycle plus the exact pinned parser showing only the live trainer. Preserve the existing GPU viewer and static stream as rollback, and roll back only by removing the entire follower service override; pairing the CPU-hiding follower with the old GPU viewer is the confirmed crash mode. After the switch, verify public HTTP/WebSocket freshness, no BBTV compute PID, unchanged primary PID/service/progress, and byte-identical primary/overflow pins. BBTV remains observational and this changes no reward, trainer, queue, scientific input, or promotion decision.

**D190 — ADD A BEHAVIOR-NEUTRAL EMITTED-REWARD COMPONENT LEDGER FOR FUTURE RUNS; DO NOT RETROFIT THE ACTIVE VACATION QUEUES (2026-07-15).** D187 could observe total reward integrity and behavior but could not say whether distance, possession, block EV, sequencing, Rush, or another term supplied the learner's return. DECISION: route every ordinary reward mutation through one attribution seam and export 28 signed episode channels from the team-0/home perspective: setup done/autofix; ball gain/loss; ball/endzone distance; injury inflicted/taken; send-off; touchback; surf inflicted/taken; combined declaration-time block exposure; block self-injury/sequence/turnover; possession; block assist; Rush; full/soft carrier exposure; carrier threat; hard/soft defensive threat; touchdown; win/loss; draw; and quarantined statmatch. Summing agents is forbidden because zero-sum channels would cancel. Components describe raw pre-clamp reward actually offered for emission; a signed clamp delta and post-clamp return preserve the PPO-visible result. A signed residual records float refolding error, while mismatch and non-finite counters fail integrity. Terminal reconstruction discards incidental same-action shaping, preserves explicit touchdown reward, and adds result/statmatch once; the ledger follows that actual emission rather than inventing counterfactual credit. The dashboard contract grows from 88 to 123 environment keys, so both vector dictionaries and the visible metric limit are raised from 96 to 160 with install/check migrations and a machine-readable contract test. Verification is behavior-locking: default 1,000-episode and R0 100-episode deterministic trajectory hashes match pristine builds (`40b99790caa43743` and `a8f086fe87ec58c8`), throughput is indistinguishable, all 431 normal and 431 ASan/UBSan C tests pass, and four Python log-contract tests pass. A real vectorized Puffer CPU smoke completed 128 eval episodes with 132 JSON fields; nonzero setup-autofix and touchback components summed to the post-clamp/episode return within float tolerance with zero mismatch/non-finite counters. Fable's headless architecture review approved the core arithmetic and its requested dashboard-capacity, call-site-label, draw/objective-bypass, and vector-path checks were resolved. This ledger enables causal diagnosis in newly built runs; it does not validate any component, alter a reward coefficient, promote R0, or support retroactive attribution. The already pinned D185/D186 vacation source, modules, plans, and queues remain byte-for-byte untouched and must not be rebuilt mid-run.

**D191 — FILTER THE HISTORICAL STATE BANK TO AN EXACT, PROVENANCE-BOUND BB2025 SUBSET BEFORE ANY REPLAY-SCENARIO WORK (2026-07-15).** The replay audit already established that loader-compatible BBS bytes do not prove source edition: the canonical 15,471-record/5,370-ID bank includes 123 records from 42 BB2020 replay IDs. A fresh polite fetch of all 42 excluded replay IDs independently confirmed embedded `rulesVersion=BB2020` for every one, with no failed fetch or unexplained exclusion. DECISION: keep `build_state_bank.py` as the from-source builder, but add a standalone streaming `tools/filter_state_bank.py` for environments where the pinned bank and strict allowlist exist but the full normalized corpus does not. It requires exact input SHA `710c7b850ad72d5d665b3ea14b93b94f5e42cb70fb1a1d5850aa39bd3d2481c5` and allowlist SHA `15d6f67852c6d556009a8f878f730c6fd6c0c45fdf77e1fd8a2b7d1b2c218585`, validates every header/meta boundary, detects concurrent input mutation, copies the count-free BBS1 header and selected opaque records byte-for-byte in order, and exclusively publishes a selected-ID list plus deterministic provenance manifest as one fail-clean same-directory transaction without overwriting a racing writer. The canonical double-run selected exactly 15,348 records from 5,328 IDs and excluded the known 123/42; output bank SHA is `bcd9daf55ac5d177f48160092f17a9b4978da877455b830ba33a9c1b5ba84d22`, selected-ID SHA is `7e22604b51010317059213f285e30a90d6f8fc2b2b358ec5d71fbcd09130c6fd`, and both reruns were byte-identical. The existing `build_state_bank.read_shard` reader accepted all 15,348 records; header, full ordered body, and first/last record comparisons were exact. Eight focused tests cover hash pins, format/metadata/allowlist failures, deterministic bytes, aliases/existing paths, no overlap, source races, exclusive publication, and injected mid-publish cleanup. This is edition hygiene only: every selected state remains half one, 12,001/15,348 are turns 1–2, only 25 reach turn 8, and replay outcomes remain invalid action-quality labels. Do not stage this bank into the active vacation build. The next separately reviewed tranche is strict-bank S1–S6 coverage classification only, followed by authored passing/handoff/second-half/score-clock/Stalling/reroll fixtures sized from the measured holes; a future from-source allowlist-at-build-time bank should supersede the filtered artifact when the full corpus is available.

**D192 — CLASSIFY STRICT-BANK S1–S6 OPPORTUNITY COVERAGE WITHOUT TURNING HISTORICAL SNAPSHOTS INTO ACTION LABELS OR TRAINING POLICY (2026-07-15).** A pure RNG-free C classifier now scans the exact D191 bank only at validated fresh-team-turn decision boundaries, and a separately hash-pinned Python layer publishes canonical JSONL, record/replay/three-per-replay-capped denominators, turn bands, overlaps, race-pair composition, and replay-ID-disjoint 70/15/15 descriptive splits through an exclusive manifest-last transaction. Raw/capped/distinct-replay counts are: S1 ball recovery `5,023/4,935/4,153`; S2 static next-turn loose contest `3,047/2,973/2,403`; S3 ordering pressure `12,661/9,961/5,322`; S4 raw own-carrier sack access `2,883/2,703/1,745`; S5 opponent-carrier one/two-turn score horizon `3,605/3,280/1,983`; and S6 fixed direct-block span or one-move zero-roll assist sensitivity `11,763/8,993/4,950`. The scanner exactly reconciles the independent pickup probe's 5,312 loose and 10,036 held states; 5,023 loose states satisfy S1 and 289 do not. Structural anomalies are zero: `S2 ⊆ S1`, `S4 ∩ S5 = ∅`, and `S6 = S6A ∪ S6B`. The report remains dominated by openings (12,001 records at turns 1–2 versus 692 at turns 5–8), so these counts can size future authored fixtures but cannot establish ordering quality, action regret, pickup/sack probability, outcome causality, or curriculum weights. S2/S4 are static opponent-next-turn geometry; S5 is straight-line horizon; S6 excludes Dauntless from fixed pool claims and only tests other-player direct blocks after one selected zero-roll move. Fable independently found and drove closure of the raw-record bounds-validation blocker, then approved the provenance/transaction layer. Normal and ASan/UBSan focused tests plus optimized and sanitized full-bank scans emit identical record bytes. DECISION: merge classification/reporting as analysis infrastructure only; do not stage this bank into the occupied vacation build, wire it into PPO/BC, use replay outcomes as labels, or smooth away the thin late-turn strata. The next data tranche is separately reviewed authored coverage for passing, handoffs, second half, score/clock, Stalling, contextual rerolls, and other holes the historical bank cannot supply.

**D193 — IMPLEMENT BB2025 STALLING AS ENGINE LAW, NOT A REWARD PENALTY (2026-07-15).** The reward/rules audit described the current Third Season rule, but a focused executable search and failing regression proved the engine never enforced it: a turn-1 carrier one free square from the end zone could end their activation standing with the ball, consumed no crowd die, and continued without a Turnover. DECISION: at carrier activation start, snapshot whether any occupied-pitch scoring path exists with zero Dodges and zero Rushes and no compulsory activation-gate, Bloodlust, Animal Savagery, or Ball & Chain die. If that player finishes the activation still standing and holding the ball without an earlier Turnover, roll a non-rerollable D6 through `bb_rng`; `D6 >= current team turn` pushes the existing `BB_KD_OTHER` chain. Voluntarily ending the team turn before activating an eligible carrier marks that carrier used and performs the same check. A prior Turnover that ends the turn first and a successful Pass/Hand-off that transfers possession are exemptions. The roll is still consumed on turns 7–8 even though it cannot succeed. Reusing KNOCKDOWN preserves one owner for Steady Footing, ball release/bounce, armour/injury, Turnover, and stack unwinding; a Steady Footing 6 therefore prevents both the knockdown and Turnover per the May 2026 FAQ. Nine behavioral tests cover the success path, turn threshold, Rush/Dodge/gate exemptions, Hand-off transfer, whole-turn forgoing, prior Turnover, and Steady Footing; a query-purity canary proves gate inspection does not mutate Skill coverage, and the touchdown canary proves a real score does not fall through into Stalling. All 411 engine, 37 reward, 2 contact-bot, and 1 loader tests pass optimized and under ASan/UBSan, and golden replay resimulation stays exact. No match field or procedure identifier was added, so the BBS1 match layout/fingerprint is unchanged. Residuals remain explicit: Fumblerooski is not implemented; Steady Footing's broader FAQ-permitted team-reroll choice is still an existing engine approximation; and the 454-way policy interface can end the whole team turn but does not yet expose the finer rulebook choice to forego only one player and continue activating others. This fix must not be deployed over the source-pinned live vacation experiment; it enters only future reviewed builds.

**D194 — AUTHOR RARE-DECISION DRILLS BY LEGAL ENGINE TRAJECTORY WITH EXACT TWO-STREAM REPLAY, NEVER BY STATE SURGERY (2026-07-15).** The strict historical bank is rich in opening opportunity states but sharply censored for Pass, Hand-off, second-half/late-drive, contextual-reroll, and score-now-versus-Stall decisions. Raw snapshots also cannot establish which continuation was good. DECISION: build a balanced authored BBS1 bank under `docs/plans/authored-drill-state-bank.md`, with procgen randomness and in-match dice treated as distinct streams. Each recipe initializes through `bb_match_init_forced_p`/`random_p`, saves the initialized raw bytes, reaches captures only through enumerated legal `bb_apply` actions, and records packed actions plus every in-match die's sides and face. Verification reruns procgen from the same seed/stream, requires initialized byte identity, scripts the game-die faces, checks decision team and legal membership before every action, requires exact dice consumption/sides, and accepts only byte-identical loader-valid decision states. Direct writes to players, grid, ball, score, turn, half, resources, status, or procedure frames are forbidden. Authored BBS metadata uses the reserved `0xA.......` source-ID namespace; train/dev/test grouping is by recipe template; counterfactual branch outcomes remain evaluation-only and never become BBS fields, observations, rewards, masks, or BC labels. The phase-1 executable proof reaches the first genuine post-kickoff team-turn with a const deterministic setup controller, rejects illegal actions, missing/extra/wrong dice, decision-team drift, initialized/captured byte drift, malformed BBS records, and is accepted byte-for-byte by the hardened Puffer loader. All 414 engine, 37 reward, 2 contact-bot, and 2 loader tests pass optimized and under ASan/UBSan. This phase proves the replay/writer boundary only; it does not yet claim F1–F5 family recipes, quota balance, sidecars, manifest-last publication, one-action continuation, or training/deployment authorization. No authored artifact may enter the occupied vacation checkout or alter either frozen queue.
